${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k}{-{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

lapse derivative:
${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

lapse evolution:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}}{-{{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}$

lapse partial evolution
${{ { \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{ { \alpha} _{,k}} _{,t}}$ ; ${{ \alpha} _{,k}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}$
${{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ a} _k}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using on lhs only ${{ a} _k} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}$
${{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
subtracting ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}$ from both sides
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}\right)} _{,k}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}{-{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}}{-{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _k} _{,m}}}} + {{{{ a} _k}} {{{{ b} ^m} _m}}}}\right)}}{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _m} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$

${{ a} _k} _{,t}$ source term: ${{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}{-{{{{ a} _k}} {{{{ b} ^m} _m}}}}$

metric evolution:
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{ \beta} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ \beta} _j} _{,i}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}}$

symmetrizing ${{ \gamma} _i} _j$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}$

${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,l}} + {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}{-{{{{{ b} ^l} _l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}} {{{{ δ} ^r} _k}}}\right)} _{,r}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}{-{{{{{ b} ^l} _l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}$ flux term: $-{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}} {{{{ δ} ^r} _k}}}\right)} _{,r}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}$ source term: ${{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}{-{{{{{ b} ^l} _l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$

Riemann curvature
${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

Ricci curvature
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{ R} ^k} _i} _k} _j}$
using ${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _k} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _j}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _j}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _m} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _i}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _i}}\right)}}\right)} _{,j}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _k}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}}}$
cancel terms using symmetries:
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _m} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _i}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _i} _m} _k}}\right)} _{,j}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}}}$
split off terms to rearrange gradient:
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l} _{,k}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p} _{,k}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{-{{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} + { {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}} + {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{ {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^p}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}}}$
combining derivatives
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + { {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}}{-{ {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^p}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}}} + {{\left( {-{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}\right)} _{,k}}}$

Gaussian curvature
${R} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ R} _i} _j}}}$
using Ricci definition
${R} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _n} _i}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}} + {{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{ d} _j} _l} _m}}\right)}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}} + {{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _n} _i}}\right)}}}} + { {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^k}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}}{-{ {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^a} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^b} ^p}} {{{{{ d} _k} _a} _b}}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}} + {{\left( {-{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}{-{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ δ} ^k} _j}}}}\right)}}}\right)} _{,k}}}\right)}}}$

${{{ Z} _k} _{,t}} = {{{-{{\left( { {-{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{ Z} _k}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{ {-{{{ \gamma} ^r} ^l}} {{{{ K} _k} _l}}} + {{{{{ δ} ^r} _k}} {{\left({{{{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}}}{-{\Theta}}}\right)}}}}\right)}}}\right)} _{,r}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{{ a} _k}} {{\left({{{{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}}}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ K} _k} _l}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{ a} _m}} + {{{{{{ d} _m} _p} _q}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ Z} _m}}}}}\right)}}}{-{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^q}} {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{{ d} _k} _p} _q}}}}{-{{{8}} {{π}} \cdot {{{ S} _k}}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{ Z} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}}}}{-{{{{ Z} _k}} {{{{ b} ^l} _l}}}}}$

		(deriv)->d_lll.x.xy += b_ul.y.x * dDelta_lll.y.xy + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.x.xy + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.x.xy + b_ul.z.x * dDelta_lll.z.xy;
		(deriv)->d_lll.x.xz += b_ul.y.x * dDelta_lll.y.xz + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.x.xz + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.x.xz + b_ul.z.x * dDelta_lll.z.xz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.x.yy += b_ul.y.x * dDelta_lll.y.yy + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.x.yy + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.x.yy + b_ul.z.x * dDelta_lll.z.yy;
		(deriv)->d_lll.x.yz += b_ul.y.x * dDelta_lll.y.yz + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.x.yz + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.x.yz + b_ul.z.x * dDelta_lll.z.yz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.x.zz += b_ul.y.x * dDelta_lll.y.zz + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.x.zz + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.x.zz + b_ul.z.x * dDelta_lll.z.zz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.y.xx += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.y.xx + b_ul.x.y * dDelta_lll.x.xx + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.y.xx + b_ul.z.y * dDelta_lll.z.xx;
		(deriv)->d_lll.y.xy += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.y.xy + b_ul.x.y * dDelta_lll.x.xy + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.y.xy + b_ul.z.y * dDelta_lll.z.xy;
		(deriv)->d_lll.y.xz += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.y.xz + b_ul.x.y * dDelta_lll.x.xz + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.y.xz + b_ul.z.y * dDelta_lll.z.xz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.y.yy += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.y.yy + b_ul.x.y * dDelta_lll.x.yy + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.y.yy + b_ul.z.y * dDelta_lll.z.yy;
		(deriv)->d_lll.y.yz += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.y.yz + b_ul.x.y * dDelta_lll.x.yz + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.y.yz + b_ul.z.y * dDelta_lll.z.yz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.y.zz += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.y.zz + b_ul.x.y * dDelta_lll.x.zz + -b_ul.z.z * dDelta_lll.y.zz + b_ul.z.y * dDelta_lll.z.zz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.z.xx += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.z.xx + b_ul.x.z * dDelta_lll.x.xx + b_ul.y.z * dDelta_lll.y.xx + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.z.xx;
		(deriv)->d_lll.z.xy += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.z.xy + b_ul.x.z * dDelta_lll.x.xy + b_ul.y.z * dDelta_lll.y.xy + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.z.xy;
		(deriv)->d_lll.z.xz += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.z.xz + b_ul.x.z * dDelta_lll.x.xz + b_ul.y.z * dDelta_lll.y.xz + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.z.xz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.z.yy += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.z.yy + b_ul.x.z * dDelta_lll.x.yy + b_ul.y.z * dDelta_lll.y.yy + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.z.yy;
		(deriv)->d_lll.z.yz += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.z.yz + b_ul.x.z * dDelta_lll.x.yz + b_ul.y.z * dDelta_lll.y.yz + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.z.yz;
		(deriv)->d_lll.z.zz += -b_ul.x.x * dDelta_lll.z.zz + b_ul.x.z * dDelta_lll.x.zz + b_ul.y.z * dDelta_lll.y.zz + -b_ul.y.y * dDelta_lll.z.zz;
		(deriv)->K_ll.xx += K_ll.xx * b_ul.x.x + -K_ll.xx * b_ul.y.y + -K_ll.xx * b_ul.z.z + 2. * K_ll.xz * b_ul.z.x + 2. * K_ll.xy * b_ul.y.x;
		(deriv)->K_ll.xy += K_ll.xx * b_ul.x.y + -K_ll.xy * b_ul.z.z + K_ll.xz * b_ul.z.y + K_ll.yz * b_ul.z.x + K_ll.yy * b_ul.y.x;
		(deriv)->K_ll.xz += K_ll.xx * b_ul.x.z + K_ll.xy * b_ul.y.z + -K_ll.xz * b_ul.y.y + K_ll.zz * b_ul.z.x + K_ll.yz * b_ul.y.x;
		(deriv)->K_ll.yy += -K_ll.yy * b_ul.x.x + K_ll.yy * b_ul.y.y + -K_ll.yy * b_ul.z.z + 2. * K_ll.yz * b_ul.z.y + 2. * K_ll.xy * b_ul.x.y;
		(deriv)->K_ll.yz += K_ll.xy * b_ul.x.z + K_ll.xz * b_ul.x.y + K_ll.yy * b_ul.y.z + K_ll.zz * b_ul.z.y + -K_ll.yz * b_ul.x.x;
		(deriv)->K_ll.zz += -K_ll.zz * b_ul.x.x + -K_ll.zz * b_ul.y.y + K_ll.zz * b_ul.z.z + 2. * K_ll.yz * b_ul.y.z + 2. * K_ll.xz * b_ul.x.z;
		(deriv)->Theta += -Theta * (b_ul.x.x + b_ul.y.y + b_ul.z.z);
		(deriv)->Z_l.x += -Z_l.x * b_ul.y.y + -Z_l.x * b_ul.z.z + Z_l.z * b_ul.z.x + Z_l.y * b_ul.y.x;
		(deriv)->Z_l.y += Z_l.x * b_ul.x.y + -Z_l.y * b_ul.x.x + Z_l.z * b_ul.z.y + -Z_l.y * b_ul.z.z;
		(deriv)->Z_l.z += Z_l.x * b_ul.x.z + Z_l.y * b_ul.y.z + -Z_l.z * b_ul.y.y + -Z_l.z * b_ul.x.x;
		(deriv)->beta_u.x += beta_u.x * b_ul.x.x + beta_u.y * b_ul.x.y + beta_u.z * b_ul.x.z + -a_u.x * tmp1 + 2. * e_u.x * tmp1 + -d_u.x * tmp1;
		(deriv)->beta_u.y += beta_u.x * b_ul.y.x + beta_u.y * b_ul.y.y + beta_u.z * b_ul.y.z + -a_u.y * tmp1 + 2. * e_u.y * tmp1 + -d_u.y * tmp1;
		(deriv)->beta_u.z += beta_u.x * b_ul.z.x + beta_u.y * b_ul.z.y + beta_u.z * b_ul.z.z + -a_u.z * tmp1 + 2. * e_u.z * tmp1 + -d_u.z * tmp1;
	}
